   var acceptButtonNode = document.querySelector('.eu-notice-action-button'); 
acceptButtonNode.addEventListener('click', function(e) { 
	e.preventDefault(); 

	var exdate=new Date();
	exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate() + 365);
	document.cookie = 'CONSENT=2;path=/;expires='+exdate.toUTCString(); 
	location.reload(); 
}); 
var eu = get_eu_c();
console.log("EUC = ", eu);
if ((eu == -1 || eu == 1) && window.location.href.indexOf("content/cookies-consent") == -1 ) {
	document.getElementById('eu-notice').className += " display";
}
  </script>
